        close[basket_for_clothes_instance,clothes_underwear]=True

behavior wash_underwear_underwater(underwear:item, sink:item):
    body:
        achieve_once inside(underwear, sink)
        # Ensure underwear is inside the sink
        achieve_once has_water(sink)
        # Ensure sink has water to wash the underwear

behavior put_in_washing_machine(underwear:item, washing_machine:item):
    body:
        achieve_once inside(underwear, washing_machine)
        # Put the underwear inside the washing machine

def has_underwear_in_sink(sink:item):
    # Function to check if there is underwear in the specified sink
    symbol has_underwear=exists o: item: (is_clothes_underwear(o) and inside(o, sink))
    return has_underwear

def has_detergent(washing_machine:item):
    # Function to check if there is detergent in the washing machine
    symbol has_detergent_inside=exists o: item : (is_detergent(o) and inside(o, washing_machine))
    return has_detergent_inside

behavior start_washing_machine(washing_machine:item):
    body:
        achieve_once closed(washing_machine) # Close the washing machine door
        achieve_once is_on(washing_machine) # Turn on the washing machine

behavior __goal__():
    body:
        bind sink: item where:
            is_sink(sink)
        bind washing_machine: item where:
            is_washing_machine(washing_machine)

        if has_underwear_in_sink(sink):
            bind underwear: item where:
                is_clothes_underwear(underwear) and inside(underwear, sink)
            wash_underwear_underwater(underwear, sink)
            put_in_washing_machine(underwear, washing_machine)

        else:
            foreach sink: item:
                if is_sink(sink) and not visited(sink):
                    observe(sink,"Check is there any underwear in the sink")

        if not has_detergent(washing_machine):
            foreach o: item:
                if is_detergent(o) and not inside(o, washing_machine):
                    achieve_once inside(o, washing_machine) # Ensure detergent is inside the washing machine

        start_washing_machine(washing_machine)

#goal_representation_end

def in_bathroom(sink:item):
    # Function to check if a sink is in the bathroom
    symbol in_bathroom= exists room: item : (is_bathroom(room) and inside(sink, room))
    return in_bathroom

behavior hand_wash_underwear(underwear:item, sink:item, soap:item):
    body:
        achieve_once inside(underwear, sink) 
        achieve has_water(sink)
        achieve_once is_clothes(underwear) 
        achieve_once is_soap(soap)
        # Place underwear in the sink and ensure the sink has water and soap is used to hand wash

behavior put_underwear_in_washing_machine(underwear:item, washing_machine:item):
    body:
        achieve_once inside(underwear, washing_machine)
        # Place the underwear in the washing machine

behavior add_detergent_and_start(washing_machine:item, detergent:item):
    body:
        achieve_once inside(detergent, washing_machine)
        achieve_once closed(washing_machine)
        achieve is_on(washing_machine)
        # Add detergent, close, and start the washing machine

behavior __goal__():
    body:
        bind sink: item where:
            is_sink(sink) and in_bathroom(sink)
        # Select a sink in the bathroom

        bind underwear: item where:
            is_clothes_underwear(underwear)
        # Select the underwear to wash

        bind soap: item where:
            is_soap(soap)
        # Select the soap to use for hand washing

        bind washing_machine: item where:
            is_washing_machine(washing_machine)
        # Select a washing machine

        bind detergent: item where:
            is_detergent(detergent)
        # Select detergent for the washing machine

        hand_wash_underwear(underwear, sink, soap)
        put_underwear_in_washing_machine(underwear, washing_machine)
        add_detergent_and_start(washing_machine, detergent)

#goal_representation_end
